30:T1f59,<h2 id="비교-연산자"><a class="heading-link" aria-hidden="true" href="#비교-연산자">비교 연산자</a></h2>
<table>
<thead>
<tr>
<th>연산자</th>
<th>설명</th>
<th>예시</th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td><code>=</code></td>
<td>같음</td>
<td><code>WHERE </code>age<code> = 25</code></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td><code>!=</code> 또는 <code>&#x3C;></code></td>
<td>같지 않음</td>
<td><code>WHERE </code>age<code> != 25</code></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td><code>&#x3C;</code></td>
<td>작음</td>
<td><code>WHERE </code>age<code> &#x3C; 25</code></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td><code>></code></td>
<td>큼</td>
<td><code>WHERE </code>age<code> > 25</code></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td><code>&#x3C;=</code></td>
<td>작거나 같음</td>
<td><code>WHERE </code>age<code> &#x3C;= 25</code></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td><code>>=</code></td>
<td>크거나 같음</td>
<td><code>WHERE </code>age<code> >= 25</code></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td><code>IS NULL</code></td>
<td>NULL 값 확인</td>
<td><code>WHERE </code>email<code> IS NULL</code></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td><code>IS NOT NULL</code></td>
<td>NULL이 아닌 값 확인</td>
<td><code>WHERE </code>email<code> IS NOT NULL</code></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td><code>BETWEEN ... AND ...</code></td>
<td>범위 내 값 확인 (양쪽 포함)</td>
<td><code>WHERE </code>age<code> BETWEEN 20 AND 30</code></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td><code>IN (...)</code></td>
<td>목록에 포함된 값 확인</td>
<td><code>WHERE </code>status<code> IN ('active', 'pending')</code></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td><code>NOT IN (...)</code></td>
<td>목록에 포함되지 않은 값 확인</td>
<td><code>WHERE </code>status<code> NOT IN ('deleted')</code></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td><code>LIKE</code></td>
<td>패턴 매칭 (부분 일치)</td>
<td><code>WHERE </code>name<code> LIKE '김%'</code></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td><code>NOT LIKE</code></td>
<td>패턴 매칭 실패</td>
<td><code>WHERE </code>name<code> NOT LIKE '김%'</code></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td><code>REGEXP</code> 또는 <code>RLIKE</code></td>
<td>정규식 매칭</td>
<td><code>WHERE </code>email<code> REGEXP '^[a-z]+@'</code></td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
<h3 id="like-패턴"><a class="heading-link" aria-hidden="true" href="#like-패턴">LIKE 패턴</a></h3>
<ul>
<li><code>%</code>: 0개 이상의 문자 (예: <code>'김%'</code> → '김'으로 시작)</li>
<li><code>_</code>: 정확히 1개의 문자 (예: <code>'김_'</code> → '김' + 1글자)</li>
</ul>
<h2 id="논리-연산자"><a class="heading-link" aria-hidden="true" href="#논리-연산자">논리 연산자</a></h2>
<table>
<thead>
<tr>
<th>연산자</th>
<th>설명</th>
<th>예시</th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td><code>AND</code> 또는 <code>&#x26;&#x26;</code></td>
<td>모든 조건이 참이어야 함</td>
<td><code>WHERE </code>age<code>> 20 AND</code>status<code> = 'active'</code></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td><code>OR</code> 또는 <code>||</code></td>
<td>하나 이상의 조건이 참이면 됨</td>
<td><code>WHERE </code>status<code>= 'active' OR</code>status<code> = 'pending'</code></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td><code>NOT</code> 또는 <code>!</code></td>
<td>조건을 반전</td>
<td><code>WHERE NOT </code>status<code> = 'deleted'</code></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td><code>XOR</code></td>
<td>하나만 참이어야 함 (둘 다 참이면 거짓)</td>
<td><code>WHERE </code>age<code>> 20 XOR</code>status<code> = 'active'</code></td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
<p><strong>우선순위</strong>: <code>NOT</code> > <code>AND</code> > <code>OR</code> > <code>XOR</code></p>
<h2 id="null-비교-주의사항"><a class="heading-link" aria-hidden="true" href="#null-비교-주의사항">NULL 비교 주의사항</a></h2>
<p><code>=</code> 연산자로는 NULL을 비교할 수 없고, <code>IS NULL</code> 또는 <code>IS NOT NULL</code>을 사용해야 한다.</p>
<figure data-rehype-pretty-code-figure=""><pre style="background-color:#1F2028;color:#c8d3f5" tabindex="0" data-language="sql" data-theme="moonlight-ii"><code data-language="sql" data-theme="moonlight-ii" style="display: grid;"><span data-line=""><span style="color:#858AA6">-- 잘못된 예시 (항상 NULL 반환)</span></span>
<span data-line=""><span style="color:#C099FF">SELECT</span><span style="color:#86E1FC"> *</span><span style="color:#C099FF"> FROM</span><span style="color:#86E1FC"> `</span><span style="color:#C3E88D">users</span><span style="color:#86E1FC">`</span><span style="color:#C099FF"> WHERE</span><span style="color:#86E1FC"> `</span><span style="color:#C3E88D">email</span><span style="color:#86E1FC">`</span><span style="color:#86E1FC"> =</span><span style="color:#C099FF"> NULL</span><span style="color:#C8D3F5">;</span></span>
<span data-line=""> </span>
